[3<font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN">注意事项](#__RefHeading__5537_848809181)</span></font>[	23](#__RefHeading__5537_848809181)

	[3.1<font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN">由于安全性考虑，合约中只能使用](#__RefHeading__5539_848809181)</span></font>[lua<font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN">中](#__RefHeading__5539_848809181)</span></font>[table<font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN">，](#__RefHeading__5539_848809181)</span></font>[math<font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN">，](#__RefHeading__5539_848809181)</span></font>[string<font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN">库，不能使用](#__RefHeading__5539_848809181)</span></font>[io<font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN">操作等。](#__RefHeading__5539_848809181)</span></font>[	23](#__RefHeading__5539_848809181)

	[3.2<font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN">脚本现在只能写在一个文件中，不支持多文件。](#__RefHeading__5541_848809181)</span></font>[	23](#__RefHeading__5541_848809181)

	[3.3<font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN">脚本大小不能超过](#__RefHeading__5543_848809181)</span></font>[64k<font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN">。](#__RefHeading__5543_848809181)</span></font>[	23](#__RefHeading__5543_848809181)

	[3.4<font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN">合约内容通过全局变量“](#__RefHeading__5545_848809181)</span></font>[contract”<font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN">传给脚本，脚本里面可以拿来就用](#__RefHeading__5545_848809181)</span></font>[	23](#__RefHeading__5545_848809181)

	[3.5<font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN">账户平衡检测开关通过在](#__RefHeading__5547_848809181)</span></font>[lua<font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN">脚本中的全局变量“](#__RefHeading__5547_848809181)</span></font>[gCheckAccount”<font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN">控制，默认关闭此开关。](#__RefHeading__5547_848809181)</span></font>[	23](#__RefHeading__5547_848809181)

	[3.6<font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN">合约内容不能超过](#__RefHeading__5549_848809181)</span></font>[4096<font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN">字节。](#__RefHeading__5549_848809181)</span></font>[	23](#__RefHeading__5549_848809181)

	[3.7<font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN">脚本中如果有异常，或逻辑不对，可以通过](#__RefHeading__5551_848809181)</span></font>[assert<font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN">，](#__RefHeading__5551_848809181)</span></font>[error<font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN">退出执行，](#__RefHeading__5551_848809181)</span></font>[lua<font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN">解释器会捕获到该异常。](#__RefHeading__5551_848809181)</span></font>[	23](#__RefHeading__5551_848809181)

	[3.8<font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN">脚本中必须以](#__RefHeading__5553_848809181)</span></font>[mylib
	= require &quot;mylib&quot;<font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN">开头，通过](#__RefHeading__5553_848809181)</span></font>[mylib<font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN">调用里面的](#__RefHeading__5553_848809181)</span></font>[API<font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN">。](#__RefHeading__5553_848809181)</span></font>[	23](#__RefHeading__5553_848809181)

## <a name="__RefHeading__5477_848809181"></a><a name="_Toc464039789"></a>
2.1 LogPrint

<center>
	<table width="664" cellpadding="7" cellspacing="0">
		<col width="21">
		<col width="29">
		<col width="279">
		<col width="278">
		<tr valign="top">
			<td colspan="2" width="64" bgcolor="#8db3e2" style="border-top: 1px solid #00000a; border-bottom: 1px solid #00000a; border-left: 1px solid #00000a; border-right: 1px solid #000001; padding-top: 0in; padding-bottom: 0in; padding-left: 0.08in; padding-right: 0.08in">

				<font color="#244061"><font face="宋体"><font size="3" style="font-size: 12pt"><span lang="zh-CN">**<font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">原型</font>**</span></font></font></font>

			</td>
			<td colspan="2" width="571" bgcolor="#ffffff" style="border: 1px solid #000001; padding-top: 0in; padding-bottom: 0in; padding-left: 0.08in; padding-right: 0.08in">

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">mylib.LogPrint(LogTable)</font></font>

			</td>
		</tr>
		<tr valign="top">
			<td colspan="2" width="64" height="17" bgcolor="#8db3e2" style="border-top: 1px solid #00000a; border-bottom: 1px solid #00000a; border-left: 1px solid #00000a; border-right: 1px solid #000001; padding-top: 0in; padding-bottom: 0in; padding-left: 0.08in; padding-right: 0.08in">

				<font color="#244061"><font face="宋体"><font size="3" style="font-size: 12pt"><span lang="zh-CN">**<font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">功能</font>**</span></font></font></font>

			</td>

			</td>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">function
				mylib_ LogPrint ()</font></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">local
				LogTable = {</font></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">		key
				= LOG_TYPE.ENUM_STRING,  --</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">日志类型</font></font></span></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">		length
				= 0,             --value</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">数据流的总长</font></font></span></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">		value
				= nil             -- </font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">字符串或数字流</font></font></span></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">}</font></font>

				<font color="#000000"> <font face="Arial, serif"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">--</font></font></font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">保存字符串</font></font></span></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">	LogTable.length
				= 9		</font></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">	LogTable.value
				= &quot;lua start&quot;</font></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">mylib.LogPrint(LogTable)</font></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">--</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">保存数据流</font></font></span></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">LogTable.key
				= LOG_TYPE.ENUM_NUMBER</font></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">	LogTable.length
				= 20		</font></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">	local
				i</font></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">	for
				i = 1,20 do</font></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">	
				    LogTable.value [i] = i</font></font>

<font color="#000000">    <font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">end</font></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">mylib.LogPrint(LogTable)</font></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">end	</font></font>

			</td>
		</tr>
	</table>
</center>

				content = {mylib.Sha256(orgContent)}</font></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">function
				mylib_Des ()</font></font>

<font color="#000000">  <font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">local
				desTbl = </font></font>

<font color="#000000">  <font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">{</font></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">	dataLen
				= 8,</font></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">	data
				= {},</font></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">	keyLen
				= 8,</font></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">	key
				= {},</font></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">	flag
				= 1</font></font>

<font color="#000000">  <font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">}</font></font>

<font color="#000000">  <font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">desTbl.data
				= {0xad, 0xdd, 0x1e, 0x1b, 0xeb, 0x8c, 0x10, 0x8d}</font></font>

<font color="#000000">  <font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">for
				i = 1,8 do</font></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">	desTbl.key[i]
				= 0x33 + i</font></font>

<font color="#000000">  <font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">end</font></font>

<font color="#000000">  </font>

<font color="#000000">  <font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">desTbl.flag
				= 0</font></font>

<font color="#000000">  </font>

<font color="#000000">  <font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">local
				content = {mylib.Des(desTbl)}</font></font>

<font color="#000000"> 
				<font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">LogPrint(LOG_TYPE.ENUM_NUMBER,#content,content)</font></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">end</font></font>

			</td>
		</tr>
	</table>

				sigTbl = </font></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">	data

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">	keyLen

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">	key
				= {},   --</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">签名公钥</font></font></span></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">	hashLen
				= 0, --</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">签名之前的</font></font></span></font><font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">hash</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">长度</font></font></span></font>

			</td>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">function
				mylib_ VerifySignature ()</font></font>

<font color="#000000">  <font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">local
				sigTbl = </font></font>

<font color="#000000">  <font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">{</font></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">	dataLen
				= 9,</font></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">	data
				= {0x31, 0x32, 0x33, 0x34, 0x35, 0x36, 0x37, 0x38, 0x39},</font></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">	keyLen
				= 33,</font></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">	key
				= {0x03, 0xee, 0xf7, 0xa3, 0x80, 0xbc, 0xf9, 0xcf, 0x97, 0x5d,
				0x91, 0x6f, 0xda, 0xb1, 0x8d, 0x08, 0x1c, 0x9d, 0x55, 0xba, 0x43,
				0x46, 0x54, 0x35, 0xa4, 0xd1, 0xcc, 0x59, 0x86, 0x10, 0xa4, 0x44,
				0x79},</font></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">	hashLen
				= 32,</font></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">	hash
				= {0x24, 0x4f, 0xa7, 0xcf, 0x97, 0xae, 0x15, 0x85, 0xd8, 0xf8,
				0x02, 0x4b, 0xa1, 0x8b, 0x8a, 0xbe, 0xce, 0x8e, 0xb9, 0xcd, 0x4d,
				0x01, 0x6d, 0xd0, 0xba, 0x8c, 0xc0, 0xdc, 0x85, 0x1a, 0x9c, 0x0e}</font></font>

<font color="#000000">  <font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">}</font></font>

<font color="#000000">  </font>

<font color="#000000">  <font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">local
				ret = mylib.VerifySignature(sigTbl)</font></font>

<font color="#000000">  <font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">if
				ret then</font></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">	LogPrint(LOG_TYPE.ENUM_STRING,string.len(&quot;ok&quot;),&quot;ok&quot;)</font></font>

<font color="#000000">  <font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">else</font></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">	LogPrint(LOG_TYPE.ENUM_STRING,string.len(&quot;bad&quot;),&quot;bad&quot;)</font></font>

<font color="#000000">  <font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">end</font></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">end</font></font>

			</td>
		</tr>
	</table>
</center>

## <a name="__RefHeading__5489_848809181"></a><a name="_Toc464039795"></a>
2.7 GetAccountPublickey

<center>
	<table width="664" cellpadding="7" cellspacing="0">
		<col width="21">
		<col width="29">
		<col width="279">
		<col width="278">
		<tr valign="top">
			<td colspan="2" width="64" bgcolor="#8db3e2" style="border-top: 1px solid #00000a; border-bottom: 1px solid #00000a; border-left: 1px solid #00000a; border-right: 1px solid #000001; padding-top: 0in; padding-bottom: 0in; padding-left: 0.08in; padding-right: 0.08in">

				<font color="#244061"><font face="宋体"><font size="3" style="font-size: 12pt"><span lang="zh-CN">**<font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">原型</font>**</span></font></font></font>

			</td>
			<td colspan="2" width="571" bgcolor="#ffffff" style="border: 1px solid #000001; padding-top: 0in; padding-bottom: 0in; padding-left: 0.08in; padding-right: 0.08in">

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">mylib.GetAccountPublickey(accountTbl[1],accountTbl[2],accountTbl[3],accountTbl[4],accountTbl[5],accountTbl[6])</font></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">function
				mylib_GetAccountPublickey()</font></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">	local
				accountTbl = {mylib.GetCurTxAccount()}</font></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">	local
				i</font></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">	local
				result =
				{mylib.GetAccountPublickey(accountTbl[1],accountTbl[2],accountTbl[3],</font></font>

<font color="#000000">             

				<font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">accountTbl[4],accountTbl[5],accountTbl[6])}</font></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">	assert(#result
				== 33,&quot;GetAccountPublickey err&quot;);</font></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">	</font></font>

<font color="#000000">    <font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">for
				i = 1,#result do</font></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">	
				 print(&quot;Publickey&quot;,i,(result[i]))</font></font>

<font color="#000000">    <font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">end</font></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">end	</font></font>

			</td>

				mylib_GetTxConFirmHeight()</font></font>

<font color="#000000">    <font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">--
				&quot;hash&quot;
				:&quot;4a2af2d83683325e780f2b859e7421f4592e3105d01017aab45c15da3910be8e&quot;</font></font>

				txhashTbl = {0x4a,0x2a,0xf2,0xd8,0x36,0x83,0x32,0x5e,</font></font>

<font color="#000000">             
				                  <font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">0x78,0x0f,0x2b,0x85,0x9e,0x74,0x21,0xf4,</font></font>

<font color="#000000">             
				                  <font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">0x59,0x2e,0x31,0x05,0xd0,0x10,0x17,0xaa,</font></font>

<font color="#000000">             
				                  <font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">0xb4,0x5c,0x15,0xda,0x39,0x10,0xbe,0x8e}</font></font>

<font color="#000000">   <font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">local
				result = mylib.GetTxConFirmHeight(unpack(txhashTbl)) </font></font>

<font color="#000000">  
				<font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">assert(result &gt;
				0,&quot;GetTxConFirmHeight err&quot;);    </font></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">end	</font></font>

				mylib_GetBlockHash()</font></font>

				height = 47037</font></font>

				i</font></font>

<font color="#000000">    <font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">local
				result = {mylib.GetBlockHash(height)}</font></font>

<font color="#000000">   
				<font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">assert(#result ==
				32,&quot;GetBlockHash err&quot;);</font></font>

<font color="#000000">    <font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">for
				i = 1,#result do</font></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">	
				 print(&quot;BlockHash&quot;,i,(result[i]))</font></font>

<font color="#000000">    <font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">end</font></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">end	</font></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">function
				mylib_WriteData()	</font></font>

<font color="#000000">   <font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">local
				writeDbTbl = {</font></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">	
				 key = &quot;config&quot;,  --</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">关键字</font></font></span></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">	
				 length = 0,  -- value</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">数据流的总长</font></font></span></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">	
				 value = {} --</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">值</font></font></span></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">	}</font></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">	addressTbl
				= {0x64,0x63,0x6D,0x43,0x62,0x4B,0x62,0x41,</font></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">					0x66,0x4B,0x72,0x6F,0x66,0x4E,0x7A,0x33,</font></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">					0x35,0x4D,0x53,0x46,0x75,0x70,0x78,0x72,</font></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">					0x78,0x34,0x55,0x77,0x6E,0x33,0x76,0x67,</font></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">					0x6A,0x4C}</font></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">	--</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">每次限额</font></font></span></font><font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">,</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">每日限额</font></font></span></font><font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">,</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">企业登记的账户地址</font></font></span></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">	writeDbTbl.value
				= {0x00,0x00,0x00,0x00,0x00,0x00,0x00,0x64,</font></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">	
				                   0x00,0x00,0x00,0x00,0x00,0x00,0x01,0x2C,</font></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">						unpack(addressTbl)}				</font></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">	writeDbTbl.length
				= #writeDbTbl.value</font></font>

<font color="#000000">   
				<font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">assert(mylib.WriteData(writeDbTbl),&quot;WriteData
				err&quot;)</font></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">end</font></font>

				<font color="#244061"><font face="宋体"><font size="3" style="font-size: 12pt"><span lang="zh-CN">**<font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">返回</font>**</span></font></font></font>

			</td>
			<td width="279" bgcolor="#ffffff" style="border: 1px solid #000001; padding-top: 0in; padding-bottom: 0in; padding-left: 0.08in; padding-right: 0.08in">

<font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">成功：</font></font></span></font><font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">true</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">；失败：</font></font></span></font><font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">false</font></font>

			</td>

				<font color="#244061"><font face="宋体"><font size="3" style="font-size: 12pt"><span lang="zh-CN">**<font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">注释</font>**</span></font></font></font>

			</td>

			</td>
		</tr>
		<tr valign="top">
			<td colspan="2" width="64" height="3" bgcolor="#8db3e2" style="border-top: 1px solid #00000a; border-bottom: 1px solid #00000a; border-left: 1px solid #00000a; border-right: 1px solid #000001; padding-top: 0in; padding-bottom: 0in; padding-left: 0.08in; padding-right: 0.08in">

				<font color="#244061"><font face="宋体"><font size="3" style="font-size: 12pt"><span lang="zh-CN">**<font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">示例</font>**</span></font></font></font>

			</td>
			<td colspan="2" width="571" bgcolor="#cccccc" style="border: 1px solid #000001; padding-top: 0in; padding-bottom: 0in; padding-left: 0.08in; padding-right: 0.08in">

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">function
				mylib_ DeleteData ()	</font></font>

<font color="#000000">   <font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">local
				writeDbTbl = {</font></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">	
				 key = &quot;config&quot;,  --</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">关键字</font></font></span></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">	
				 length = 0,  -- value</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">数据流的总长</font></font></span></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">	
				 value = {} --</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">值</font></font></span></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">	}</font></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">	assert(mylib.DeleteData(writeDbTbl.key),&quot;DeleteData
				err&quot;)</font></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">	print(&quot;DeleteData
				return ok&quot;)</font></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">	local
				readResult = {}</font></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">	readResult
				=  {mylib.ReadData(writeDbTbl.key)}	</font></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">	if(TableIsEmpty(readResult))
				then</font></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">		print(&quot;DeleteData
				ok&quot;)</font></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">	end	</font></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">end</font></font>

			</td>
		</tr>
	</table>
</center>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">function
				mylib_ ReadData ()	</font></font>

<font color="#000000">   <font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">local
				key =“config”</font></font>

<font color="#000000">   <font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">local
				readResult =  {mylib.ReadData(key)}	</font></font>

<font color="#000000">  
				<font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">assert(#readResult &gt;
				0,&quot;ReadData0 err&quot;)</font></font>

<font color="#000000">   <font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">local
				i</font></font>

<font color="#000000">   <font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">for
				i = 1,#readResult do</font></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">	print(&quot;&quot;,i,(readResult[i]))</font></font>

<font color="#000000">  <font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">end
				</font></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">end</font></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">function
				mylib_ ModifyData ()	</font></font>

<font color="#000000">   <font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">local
				writeDbTbl = {</font></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">	
				 key = &quot;config&quot;,  --</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">关键字</font></font></span></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">	
				 length = 0,  -- value</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">数据流的总长</font></font></span></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">	
				 value = {} --</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">值</font></font></span></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">	}</font></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">	addressTbl
				= {0x64,0x63,0x6D,0x43,0x62,0x4B,0x62,0x41,</font></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">					0x66,0x4B,0x72,0x6F,0x66,0x4E,0x7A,0x33,</font></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">					0x35,0x4D,0x53,0x46,0x75,0x70,0x78,0x72,</font></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">					0x78,0x34,0x55,0x77,0x6E,0x33,0x76,0x67,</font></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">					0x6A,0x4C}</font></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">	--</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">每次限额</font></font></span></font><font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">,</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">每日限额</font></font></span></font><font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">,</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">企业登记的账户地址</font></font></span></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">	writeDbTbl.value
				= {0x00,0x00,0x00,0x00,0x00,0x00,0x00,0x64,</font></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">	
				                   0x00,0x00,0x00,0x00,0x00,0x00,0x01,0x2C,</font></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">						unpack(addressTbl)}			</font></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">	writeDbTbl.length
				= #writeDbTbl.value</font></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">	writeDbTbl.value[8]
				= 200</font></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">	assert(mylib.ModifyData(writeDbTbl),&quot;ModifyData
				err&quot;)</font></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">	print(&quot;ModifyData
				ok&quot;)</font></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">	readResult
				= {}</font></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">	readResult
				=  {mylib.ReadData(writeDbTbl.key)}	</font></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">	assert(#readResult
				&gt; 0,&quot;ReadData1 err&quot;)</font></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">	print(&quot;ReadData1
				ok&quot;)</font></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">	for
				i = 1,#readResult do</font></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">		print(&quot;&quot;,i,(readResult[i]))</font></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">	end
				</font></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">end</font></font>

			</td>
		</tr>
	</table>
</center>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">function
				WriteWithDrawal(accTbl,moneyTbl)</font></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">		--</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">执行系统账户提现操作</font></font></span></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">		assert(TableIsNotEmpty(accTbl),&quot;WriteWithDrawal
				accTbl invlaid1&quot;)</font></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">		assert(TableIsNotEmpty
				(moneyTbl),&quot;WriteWithDrawal moneyTbl invlaid1&quot;)	</font></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">	</font></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">		local
				writeOutputTbl = {</font></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">			addrType
				= 1,      --</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">账户类型
				</font></font></span></font><font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">REG_ID
				= 0x01,BASE_58_ADDR = 0x02,</font></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">			accountIdTbl
				= {},   --account id</font></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">			operatorType
				= 0,   --</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">操作类型</font></font></span></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">			outHeight
				= 0,     --</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">超时高度</font></font></span></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">			moneyTbl
				= {}      --</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">金额</font></font></span></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">		}		</font></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">		</font></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">		writeOutputTbl.accountIdTbl
				= {unpack(accTbl)}</font></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">		writeOutputTbl.operatorType
				= OPER_TYPE.</font></font> <font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">ENUM_ADD_FREE</font></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">		writeOutputTbl.moneyTbl
				= {unpack(moneyTbl)}</font></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">		assert(mylib.WriteOutput(writeOutputTbl),&quot;WriteWithDrawal
				WriteOutput err0&quot;)</font></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">		</font></font>

<font color="#000000">        
				<font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">writeOutputTbl.operatorType
				= OPER_TYPE.</font></font> <font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">ENUM_MINUS_FREE</font></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">	
				   writeOutputTbl.accountidTbl = {mylib.GetScriptID()}</font></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">	
				   assert(mylib.WriteOutput(writeOutputTbl),&quot;WriteWithDrawal
				WriteOutput err1&quot;)</font></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">	end</font></font>

			</td>
		</tr>
	</table>
</center>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">function
				mylib_GetScriptData()</font></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">	mylib_WriteData()</font></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">	local
				paraTbl = {</font></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">	
				 --id = {0x00,0x01,0x00,0x00,0xb7,0xc4}, --6</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">字节的脚本</font></font></span></font><font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">id</font></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">	
				 id = {mylib.GetScriptID()},</font></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">	
				 key = &quot;config&quot;,      --</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">关键字</font></font></span></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">	}</font></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">	local
				result = {mylib.GetScriptData(paraTbl)}</font></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">	assert(#result
				&gt; 0,&quot;GetScriptData err&quot;)</font></font>

<font color="#000000">    <font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">for
				i = 1,#result do</font></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">	
				 print(&quot;GetScriptData&quot;,i,(result[i]))</font></font>

<font color="#000000">    <font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">end</font></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">end	</font></font>

			</td>
		</tr>
	</table>

				mylib_GetScriptID()  </font></font>

				result = {mylib. GetScriptID ())}</font></font>

				&gt; 0,&quot; GetScriptID err&quot;)</font></font>

				i = 1,#result do</font></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">	
				 print(&quot;GetScriptID&quot;,i,(result[i]))</font></font>

<font color="#000000">    <font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">end</font></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">function
				mylib_ GetUserAppAccValue ()</font></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">	local
				idTbl = {</font></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">		idlen
				= 6,       --id</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">长度</font></font></span></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">		idValueTbl
				= {0x01,0x02,0x03,0x04,0x05,0x06}	 --id</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">值</font></font></span></font><font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">	</font></font>

<font color="#000000">    <font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">}</font></font>

<font color="#000000">    <font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">local
				i</font></font>

<font color="#000000">    <font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">local
				money = { mylib.GetUserAppAccValue(idTbl) }</font></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">	assert(#money
				 == 8,&quot; GetUserAppAccValue err&quot;);</font></font>

<font color="#000000">    <font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">for
				i = 1,# money do</font></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">	
				 print(&quot;money &quot;,i,( money [i]))</font></font>

<font color="#000000">    <font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">end</font></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">end	</font></font>

			</td>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">function
				mylib_GetBase58Addr()</font></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">	local
				accountTbl = {5,157,0,0,7,34}    --6</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">字节的账户</font></font></span></font><font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">ID</font></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">							</font></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">	local
				result = {mylib.GetBase58Addr(unpack(accountTbl))}</font></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">	assert(#result
				&gt; 0,&quot;GetBase58Addr err&quot;)	</font></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">	if(#result
				&gt; 0) then</font></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">		LogPrint(LOG_TYPE.NUMBER,#result,result)	</font></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">	end	</font></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">end</font></font>

			</td>
		</tr>
	</table>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">function
				mylib_IntegerToByte()</font></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">	local
				height =  1440</font></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">	local
				result = {mylib.IntegerToByte4(height)}</font></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">	assert(#result
				== 4,&quot;IntegerToByte4 error0&quot;)</font></font>

<font color="#000000">    <font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">local
				i</font></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">	print(&quot;height
				byte&quot;)	</font></font>

<font color="#000000">    <font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">for
				i = 1,#result do</font></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">	
				 print(&quot;&quot;,i,(result[i]))</font></font>

<font color="#000000">    <font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">end</font></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">end</font></font>

			</td>

				<font color="#244061"><font face="宋体"><font size="3" style="font-size: 12pt"><span lang="zh-CN">**<font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">注释</font>**</span></font></font></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">function
				mylib_TransferContactAsset()</font></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">	local
				accountTbl = {5,157,0,0,7,34}    --6</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">字节的账户</font></font></span></font><font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">ID</font></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">							</font></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">	local
				addrTbl = {mylib.GetBase58Addr(unpack(accountTbl))}</font></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">	assert(#addrTbl
				&gt; 0,&quot;GetBase58Addr err&quot;)	</font></font>

<font color="#000000">   
				<font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">assert(mylib.TransferContactAsset(Unpack(addrTbl)),
				&quot;TransferContactAsset err&quot;)</font></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">end</font></font>

			</td>

				<font color="#244061"><font face="宋体"><font size="3" style="font-size: 12pt"><span lang="zh-CN">**<font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">示例</font>**</span></font></font></font>

			</td>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">function
				mylib_TransferSomeAsset()</font></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">	local
				accountTbl = {5,157,0,0,7,34}    --6</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">字节的账户</font></font></span></font><font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">ID</font></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">							</font></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">	local
				addrTbl = {mylib.GetBase58Addr(unpack(accountTbl))}</font></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">	assert(#addrTbl
				&gt; 0,&quot;GetBase58Addr err&quot;)	</font></font>

<font color="#000000">    <font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">local
				assetOperateTbl = {</font></font>

<font color="#000000">    <font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">toAddrTbl
				= {}, --</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">转移地址</font></font></span></font>

<font color="#000000">  <font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">	outHeight
				= 0,  --</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">高度
				</font></font></span></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">	moneyTbl
				= {},  --</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">资产数</font></font></span></font>

<font color="#000000">   
				<font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">fundTagLen = 0,   --fund
				tag len</font></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">	fundTagTbl
				= {}   --fund tag </font></font>

<font color="#000000">  <font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">}</font></font>

<font color="#000000">  <font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">local
				money =  1311768465173141112</font></font>

<font color="#000000">  <font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">local
				moneyTbl = {mylib.IntegerToByte8(money)}</font></font>

<font color="#000000"> 
				<font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">assetOperateTbl.toAddrTbl =
				addrTbl</font></font>

<font color="#000000"> 
				<font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">assetOperateTbl.outHeight =
				1440</font></font>

<font color="#000000"> 
				<font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">assetOperateTbl.moneyTbl =
				moneyTbl</font></font>

<font color="#000000"> 
				<font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">assert(mylib.TransferSomeAsset(assetOperateTbl),
				&quot;TransferSomeAsset err&quot;)</font></font>

<font color="#000000"><font size="2" style="font-size: 9pt">end</font></font>

			</td>
		</tr>
	</table>
</center>

## <a name="__RefHeading__5539_848809181"></a><a name="_Toc464039820"></a>
3.1<font face="华文楷体"><span lang="zh-CN">由于安全性考虑，合约中只能使用</span></font>lua<font face="华文楷体"><span lang="zh-CN">中</span></font>table<font face="华文楷体"><span lang="zh-CN">，</span></font>math<font face="华文楷体"><span lang="zh-CN">，</span></font>string<font face="华文楷体"><span lang="zh-CN">库，不能使用</span></font>io<font face="华文楷体"><span lang="zh-CN">操作等。</span></font>

## <a name="__RefHeading__5541_848809181"></a><a name="_Toc464039821"></a>
3.2<font face="华文楷体"><span lang="zh-CN">脚本现在只能写在一个文件中，不支持多文件。</span></font>

## <a name="__RefHeading__5543_848809181"></a><a name="_Toc464039822"></a>
3.3<font face="华文楷体"><span lang="zh-CN">脚本大小不能超过</span></font>64k<font face="华文楷体"><span lang="zh-CN">。</span></font>

## <a name="__RefHeading__5545_848809181"></a><a name="_Toc464039823"></a>
3.4<font face="华文楷体"><span lang="zh-CN">合约内容通过全局变量“</span></font>contract”<font face="华文楷体"><span lang="zh-CN">传给脚本，脚本里面可以拿来就用</span></font>

## <a name="__RefHeading__5547_848809181"></a><a name="_Toc464039824"></a>
3.5<font face="华文楷体"><span lang="zh-CN">账户平衡检测开关通过在</span></font>lua<font face="华文楷体"><span lang="zh-CN">脚本中的全局变量“</span></font>gCheckAccount”<font face="华文楷体"><span lang="zh-CN">控制，默认关闭此开关。</span></font>

## <a name="__RefHeading__5549_848809181"></a><a name="_Toc464039825"></a>
3.6<font face="华文楷体"><span lang="zh-CN">合约内容不能超过</span></font>4096<font face="华文楷体"><span lang="zh-CN">字节。</span></font>

## <a name="__RefHeading__5551_848809181"></a><a name="_Toc464039826"></a>
3.7<font face="华文楷体"><span lang="zh-CN">脚本中如果有异常，或逻辑不对，可以通过</span></font>assert<font face="华文楷体"><span lang="zh-CN">，</span></font>error<font face="华文楷体"><span lang="zh-CN">退出执行，</span></font>lua<font face="华文楷体"><span lang="zh-CN">解释器会捕获到该异常。</span></font>

## <a name="__RefHeading__5553_848809181"></a><a name="_Toc464039827"></a>
3.8<font face="华文楷体"><span lang="zh-CN">脚本中必须以</span></font>mylib
= require &quot;mylib&quot;<font face="华文楷体"><span lang="zh-CN">开头，通过</span></font>mylib<font face="华文楷体"><span lang="zh-CN">调用里面的</span></font>API<font face="华文楷体"><span lang="zh-CN">。</span></font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">mylib
= require &quot;mylib&quot;</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">--</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">日志类型</font></span></font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">LOG_TYPE
= </font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">{</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">ENUM_STRING = 0, --</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">字符串类型</font></span></font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">ENUM_NUMBER = 1, --</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">数字类型
</font></span></font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">};</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">--</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">系统账户操作定义</font></span></font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">OPER_TYPE
= </font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">{</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	ENUM_ADD_FREE
= 1,   --</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">系统账户加</font></span></font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	ENUM_MINUS_FREE
= 2  --</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">系统账户减</font></span></font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">}</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">--</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">脚本应用账户操作类型定义</font></span></font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">APP_OPERATOR_TYPE
= </font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">{
</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	ENUM_ADD_FREE_OP
= 1,      --</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">自由账户加</font></span></font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	ENUM_SUB_FREE_OP
= 2,      --</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">自由账户减</font></span></font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	ENUM_ADD_FREEZED_OP
= 3,   --</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">冻结账户加</font></span></font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	ENUM_SUB_FREEZED_OP
= 4    --</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">冻结账户减</font></span></font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">}</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">--</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">账户类型</font></span></font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">ADDR_TYPE
= </font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">{</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	ENUM_REGID
= 1,		-- REG_ID</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	ENUM_BASE58
= 2,	-- BASE58 ADDR</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">}</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">--</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">交易类型</font></span></font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">TX_TYPE
= </font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">{</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	TX_WITHDRAW
= 1,	--</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">提现</font></span></font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	TX_RECHARGE=
2, 	--</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">充值</font></span></font><font face="华文楷体, serif">	
</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">}</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">FREEZE_MONTH_NUM
= 20   	-- </font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">冻结次数</font></span></font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">FREEZE_PERIOD
= 5	-- </font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">冻结周期</font></span></font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">MAX_MONEY
= 100000000000000000 -- </font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">总金额限制</font></span></font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">FREE_MONEY
= 10000000000000000 -- </font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">自由金额限制</font></span></font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">gCheckAccount
= true -- </font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">平衡检查
</font></span></font><font face="华文楷体, serif">true </font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">打开，</font></span></font><font face="华文楷体, serif">false
</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">关闭</font></span></font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">gSendAccountTbl
= 			-- </font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">发币地址</font></span></font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">{</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	0x00,
0x00, 0x00, 0x00, 0x01, 0x00</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">}</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">--</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">判断表是否为空</font></span></font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">function
TableIsEmpty(t)</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	return
_G.next(t) == nil</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">end</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">--</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">判断表非空</font></span></font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">function
TableIsNotEmpty(t)</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">return false == TableIsEmpty(t)</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">end</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">--[[</font>

<font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">功能</font></span></font><font face="华文楷体, serif">:</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">日志输出</font></span></font>

  <font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">参数：</font></span></font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	aKey:</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">日志类型</font></span></font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	bLength:</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">日志长度</font></span></font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	cValue</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">：日志</font></span></font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">--]]</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">function
LogPrint(aKey,bLength,cValue)</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	assert(bLength
&gt;= 1,&quot;LogPrint bLength invlaid&quot;)</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	if(aKey
== LOG_TYPE.ENUM_STRING) then  </font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">assert(type(cValue) ==
&quot;string&quot;,&quot;LogPrint cValue invlaid0&quot;)</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	elseif(aKey
== LOG_TYPE.ENUM_NUMBER)	 then	   </font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	
   assert(TableIsNotEmpty(cValue),&quot;LogPrint cValue invlaid1&quot;)</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	else</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	
   error(&quot;LogPrint aKey invlaid&quot;) </font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	end	</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	local
logTable = {</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">		key
= LOG_TYPE.ENUM_STRING,  </font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">		length
= 0,             </font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">		value
= nil             </font>

    <font face="华文楷体, serif">}</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	logTable.key
= aKey </font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	logTable.length
= bLength		</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	logTable.value
= cValue</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	mylib.LogPrint(logTable)</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">end</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">--[[</font>

<font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">功能</font></span></font><font face="华文楷体, serif">:</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">遍历表元素</font></span></font>

  <font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">参数：</font></span></font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	t:</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">表</font></span></font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	i:</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">开始索引</font></span></font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">--]]</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">function
Unpack(t,i)</font>

   <font face="华文楷体, serif">i
= i or 1</font>

   <font face="华文楷体, serif">if
t[i] then</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">return t[i],Unpack(t,i+1)</font>

   <font face="华文楷体, serif">end</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">end</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">--[[</font>

<font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">功能</font></span></font><font face="华文楷体, serif">:</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">比较两表元素是否相同</font></span></font>

  <font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">参数：</font></span></font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	tDest:</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">表</font></span></font><font face="华文楷体, serif">1</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	tSrc:</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">表</font></span></font><font face="华文楷体, serif">2</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	start1:</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">开始索引</font></span></font>

  <font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">返回值：</font></span></font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	0:</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">相等</font></span></font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	1:</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">表</font></span></font><font face="华文楷体, serif">1&gt;</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">表</font></span></font><font face="华文楷体, serif">2</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	2:</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">表</font></span></font><font face="华文楷体, serif">1&lt;</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">表</font></span></font><font face="华文楷体, serif">2</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">--]]</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">function
MemCmp(tDest,tSrc,start1)</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	assert(TableIsNotEmpty(tDest),&quot;tDest
is empty&quot;)</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	assert(TableIsNotEmpty(tSrc),&quot;tSrc
is empty&quot;)</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	local
i </font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	for
i = #tDest,1,-1 do </font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">		if
tDest[i] &gt; tSrc[i + start1 - 1] then </font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">			return
1  </font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">		elseif
	tDest[i] &lt; tSrc[i + start1 - 1] then</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">			return
-1 </font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">		else
</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">		</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">		end</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	end</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	return
0 </font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">end</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">--[[</font>

<font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">功能</font></span></font><font face="华文楷体, serif">:</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">获取表从开始索引指定长度的元素集合</font></span></font>

  <font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">参数：</font></span></font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	tbl:</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">表</font></span></font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	start:</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">开始索引</font></span></font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	length:</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">长度</font></span></font>

  <font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">返回值：</font></span></font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">一个新表</font></span></font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">--]]</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">function
GetValueFromContract(tbl,start,length)</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">assert(start &gt;
0,&quot;GetValueFromContract start err&quot;)</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">assert(length &gt;
0,&quot;GetValueFromContract length err&quot;)</font>

  <font face="华文楷体, serif">local
newTab = {}</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	local
i</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	for
i = 0,length -1 do</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">		newTab[1
+ i] = tbl[start + i]</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	end</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">return newTab</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">end</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">--[[</font>

  <font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">功能</font></span></font><font face="华文楷体, serif">:</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">充值</font></span></font>

  <font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">参数：</font></span></font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">无</font></span></font>

  <font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">返回值：</font></span></font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	true:</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">成功</font></span></font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	false:</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">失败</font></span></font>

  <font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">流程：</font></span></font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	1</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">）获取当前交易账户，并判断是否与发币地址一致</font></span></font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	2</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">）获取合约相应内容，并判断合法性</font></span></font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	3</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">）将自由金额提现到系统账户下</font></span></font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	4</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">）冻结相应的冻结部分</font></span></font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	5</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">）扣除相应的脚本账户下的金额</font></span></font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">--]]</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">function
Recharge()</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	--
1</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">）</font></span></font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	--
local accountTbl = {0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0}</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	--
accountTbl = {mylib.GetCurTxAccount()}</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	--
assert(TableIsNotEmpty(accountTbl),&quot;GetCurTxAccount error&quot;)</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	--
assert(MemCmp(gSendAccountTbl, accountTbl,1) == 0,&quot;Recharge
address err&quot;)</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	--
2</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">）</font></span></font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	local
toAddrTbl = {}</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	toAddrTbl
= GetValueFromContract(contract, 3, 34)</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	local
moneyTbl = {}</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	moneyTbl
= GetValueFromContract(contract, 37, 8)  </font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">local money =
mylib.ByteToInteger(Unpack(moneyTbl))</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	assert(money
&gt; 0,&quot;money &lt;= 0&quot;)</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	local
freeMoneyTbl = {}</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	freeMoneyTbl
= GetValueFromContract(contract, 45, 8)  </font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">local freeMoney =
mylib.ByteToInteger(Unpack(freeMoneyTbl))</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	assert(freeMoney
&gt; 0,&quot;freeMoney &lt;= 0&quot;)</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	local
freeMonthMoneyTbl = {}</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	freeMonthMoneyTbl
= GetValueFromContract(contract, 53, 8)  </font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">local freeMonthMoney =
mylib.ByteToInteger(Unpack(freeMonthMoneyTbl))</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	assert(freeMonthMoney
&gt; 0,&quot;freeMonthMoney &lt;= 0&quot;)</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	local
payMoneyTbl = {}</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	payMoneyTbl
= {mylib.GetCurTxPayAmount()}</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	assert(TableIsNotEmpty(payMoneyTbl),&quot;GetCurTxPayAmount
error&quot;)</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	local
payMoney = mylib.ByteToInteger(Unpack(payMoneyTbl))</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	assert(payMoney
&gt; 0,&quot;payMoney &lt;= 0&quot;)</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	--
</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">总金额与充值金额要相等</font></span></font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	assert(money
== payMoney, &quot;</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">充值金额不正确</font></span></font><font face="华文楷体, serif">1&quot;)</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	--
</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">总金额不能小于</font></span></font><font face="华文楷体, serif">1,</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">不能小于自由金额或月冻结金额</font></span></font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	if
money &lt; 1 </font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">		or
money &lt; freeMoney </font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">		or
money &lt; freeMonthMoney then</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">		LogPrint(LOG_TYPE.ENUM_STRING,
string.len(&quot;</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">充值金额不正确</font></span></font><font face="华文楷体, serif">2&quot;),
&quot;</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">充值金额不正确</font></span></font><font face="华文楷体, serif">2&quot;);</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">		error(&quot;</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">充值金额不正确</font></span></font><font face="华文楷体, serif">2&quot;)</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	end</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	--
</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">三个金额，上限值检测</font></span></font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	if
money &gt;= MAX_MONEY </font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">		or
freeMoney &gt;= FREE_MONEY</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">		or
freeMonthMoney &gt;= FREE_MONEY then</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">		LogPrint(LOG_TYPE.ENUM_STRING,
string.len(&quot;</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">充值金额不正确</font></span></font><font face="华文楷体, serif">3&quot;),
&quot;</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">充值金额不正确</font></span></font><font face="华文楷体, serif">3&quot;);</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">		error(&quot;</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">充值金额不正确</font></span></font><font face="华文楷体, serif">3&quot;)</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	end</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	local
freezeNum = FREEZE_MONTH_NUM - 1</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	assert(freezeNum
&gt; 0, &quot;</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">月冻结总数不正确</font></span></font><font face="华文楷体, serif">&quot;)</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	--
</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">总金额不能小于总的月冻结金额</font></span></font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	local
freezeMoney = freeMonthMoney * freezeNum</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	if
 freezeMoney &lt; freezeNum</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">		or
freezeMoney &lt; freeMoney </font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">		or
money &lt; freezeMoney then</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">		LogPrint(LOG_TYPE.ENUM_STRING,
string.len(&quot;</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">充值金额不正确</font></span></font><font face="华文楷体, serif">4&quot;),
&quot;</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">充值金额不正确</font></span></font><font face="华文楷体, serif">4&quot;);</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">		error(&quot;</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">充值金额不正确</font></span></font><font face="华文楷体, serif">4&quot;)</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	end</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	--
</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">检查充值总金额和自由金额加上冻结金额是否相等</font></span></font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	freezeMoney
= freezeMoney + freeMoney</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	if
money ~= freezeMoney then</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">		LogPrint(LOG_TYPE.ENUM_STRING,
string.len(&quot;</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">充值金额不正确</font></span></font><font face="华文楷体, serif">5&quot;),
&quot;</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">充值金额不正确</font></span></font><font face="华文楷体, serif">5&quot;);</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">		error(&quot;</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">充值金额不正确</font></span></font><font face="华文楷体, serif">5&quot;)</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	end</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	--
3</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">）</font></span></font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	--</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">操作系统账户的结构</font></span></font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	local
writeOutputTbl = </font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	{</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">		addrType
= 1,       --</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">账户类型
</font></span></font><font face="华文楷体, serif">REG_ID =
0x01,BASE_58_ADDR = 0x02,</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">		accountIdTbl
= {},  --account id</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">		operatorType
= 0,   --</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">操作类型</font></span></font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">		outHeight
= 0,      --</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">超时高度</font></span></font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">		moneyTbl
= {}       --</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">金额</font></span></font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	}</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	writeOutputTbl.addrType
= ADDR_TYPE.ENUM_BASE58</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	writeOutputTbl.operatorType
= OPER_TYPE.ENUM_ADD_FREE</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	writeOutputTbl.accountIdTbl
= {Unpack(toAddrTbl)}</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	writeOutputTbl.moneyTbl
= {Unpack(freeMoneyTbl)}</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	assert(mylib.WriteOutput(writeOutputTbl),&quot;WriteOutput
err1&quot;)</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	local
curHeight = 0</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">curHeight =
mylib.GetCurRunEnvHeight()</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	--
4</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">）</font></span></font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	local
appOperateTbl = {</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">		operatorType
= 0, -- </font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">操作类型</font></span></font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">		outHeight
= 0,    -- </font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">超时高度</font></span></font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">		moneyTbl
= {},    </font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">		userIdLen
= 0,    -- </font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">地址长度</font></span></font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">		userIdTbl
= {},   -- </font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">地址</font></span></font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">		fundTagLen
= 0,   -- fund tag len</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">		fundTagTbl
= {}   -- fund tag </font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	}
</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	appOperateTbl.operatorType
= APP_OPERATOR_TYPE.ENUM_ADD_FREEZED_OP</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">appOperateTbl.userIdLen = 34</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">appOperateTbl.userIdTbl = toAddrTbl</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">appOperateTbl.moneyTbl =
freeMonthMoneyTbl</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	for
i = 1, freezeNum do </font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">appOperateTbl.outHeight = curHeight
+ FREEZE_PERIOD * i</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">assert(mylib.WriteOutAppOperate(appOperateTbl),&quot;WriteOutAppOperate
err1&quot;)</font>

    <font face="华文楷体, serif">end</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	--
5</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">）</font></span></font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	writeOutputTbl.addrType
= ADDR_TYPE.ENUM_REGID</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	writeOutputTbl.operatorType
= OPER_TYPE.ENUM_MINUS_FREE</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	writeOutputTbl.accountIdTbl
= {mylib.GetScriptID()}</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	assert(mylib.WriteOutput(writeOutputTbl),&quot;WriteOutput
err2&quot;)</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	return
true</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">end</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">--[[</font>

<font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">功能</font></span></font><font face="华文楷体, serif">:</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">操作系统账户</font></span></font>

  <font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">参数：</font></span></font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	accTbl:</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">账户</font></span></font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	moneyTbl:</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">操作金额</font></span></font>

  <font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">返回值：</font></span></font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	true:</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">成功</font></span></font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	false:</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">失败</font></span></font>

  <font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">流程：</font></span></font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	1</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">）增加该系统账户金额</font></span></font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	2</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">）相应地减少脚本账户金额</font></span></font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">--]]</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">function
WriteWithdrawal(accTbl,moneyTbl)</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	--</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">操作系统账户的结构</font></span></font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	local
writeOutputTbl = </font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	{</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">		addrType
= 1,       --</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">账户类型
</font></span></font><font face="华文楷体, serif">REG_ID =
0x01,BASE_58_ADDR = 0x02,</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">		accountIdTbl
= {},  --account id</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">		operatorType
= 0,   --</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">操作类型</font></span></font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">		outHeight
= 0,      --</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">超时高度</font></span></font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">		moneyTbl
= {}       --</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">金额</font></span></font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	}	</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	--</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">执行系统账户提现操作</font></span></font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	assert(TableIsNotEmpty(accTbl),&quot;WriteWithDrawal
accTbl invlaid1&quot;)</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	assert(TableIsNotEmpty(moneyTbl),&quot;WriteWithDrawal
moneyTbl invlaid1&quot;)	</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	--
1</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">）</font></span></font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	writeOutputTbl.addrType
= ADDR_TYPE.ENUM_REGID</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	writeOutputTbl.operatorType
= OPER_TYPE.ENUM_ADD_FREE</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	writeOutputTbl.accountIdTbl
= {Unpack(accTbl)}</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	writeOutputTbl.moneyTbl
= {Unpack(moneyTbl)}</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	assert(mylib.WriteOutput(writeOutputTbl),&quot;WriteWithDrawal
WriteOutput err0&quot;)</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	--
2</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">）</font></span></font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	writeOutputTbl.operatorType
= OPER_TYPE.ENUM_MINUS_FREE</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	writeOutputTbl.accountIdTbl
= {mylib.GetScriptID()}</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	assert(mylib.WriteOutput(writeOutputTbl),&quot;WriteWithDrawal
WriteOutput err1&quot;)</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	return
true</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">end	</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">--[[</font>

  <font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">功能</font></span></font><font face="华文楷体, serif">:</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">提现</font></span></font>

  <font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">参数：</font></span></font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	addrType:</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">账户类型，</font></span></font><font face="华文楷体, serif">BASE58</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">或</font></span></font><font face="华文楷体, serif">REGID</font>

  <font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">返回值：</font></span></font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	true:</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">成功</font></span></font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	false:</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">失败</font></span></font>

  <font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">流程：</font></span></font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	1</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">）判断账户类型</font></span></font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	2</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">）获取当前交易账户</font></span></font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	3</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">）获取该账户下的自由金额</font></span></font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	4</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">）减掉该账户下的自由金额</font></span></font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	5</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">）相应的操作系统账户</font></span></font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">--]]</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">function
Withdraw(addrType)</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	--
1</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">）</font></span></font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	if
addrType ~= ADDR_TYPE.ENUM_REGID and addrType ~=
ADDR_TYPE.ENUM_BASE58 then</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">		error(&quot;In
function Withdraw, addr type err&quot;)</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	end</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	--
2</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">）</font></span></font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	local
accountTbl = {0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0}</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	accountTbl
= {mylib.GetCurTxAccount()}</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	assert(TableIsNotEmpty(accountTbl),&quot;GetCurTxAccount
error&quot;)</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	local
idTbl = </font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	{</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">		idLen
= 0,       </font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">		idValueTbl
= {}	 </font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	}</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	if
addrType == ADDR_TYPE.ENUM_REGID then</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">		idTbl.idLen
= 6</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">		idTbl.idValueTbl
= accountTbl</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	else</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">		local
base58Addr = {}</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">		base58Addr
= {mylib.GetBase58Addr(Unpack(accountTbl))}</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">		assert(TableIsNotEmpty(base58Addr),&quot;GetBase58Addr
error&quot;)</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">		idTbl.idLen
= 34</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">		idTbl.idValueTbl
= base58Addr</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	end</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	--
3</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">）</font></span></font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	local
freeMoneyTbl = {mylib.GetUserAppAccValue(idTbl)}</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	assert(TableIsNotEmpty(freeMoneyTbl),&quot;GetUserAppAccValue
error&quot;)</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	local
freeMoney = mylib.ByteToInteger(Unpack(freeMoneyTbl))</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	assert(freeMoney
&gt; 0,&quot;Account balance is 0.&quot;)</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	--
4</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">）</font></span></font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	local
appOperateTbl = {</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">		operatorType
= 0, -- </font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">操作类型</font></span></font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">		outHeight
= 0,    -- </font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">超时高度</font></span></font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">		moneyTbl
= {},    </font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">		userIdLen
= 0,    -- </font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">地址长度</font></span></font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">		userIdTbl
= {},   -- </font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">地址</font></span></font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">		fundTagLen
= 0,   -- fund tag len</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">		fundTagTbl
= {}   -- fund tag </font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	}
</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">appOperateTbl.operatorType =
APP_OPERATOR_TYPE.ENUM_SUB_FREE_OP</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">appOperateTbl.userIdLen =
idTbl.idLen</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">appOperateTbl.userIdTbl =
idTbl.idValueTbl</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">appOperateTbl.moneyTbl =
freeMoneyTbl</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">assert(mylib.WriteOutAppOperate(appOperateTbl),&quot;WriteOutAppOperate
err1&quot;)</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	--
5</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">）</font></span></font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	assert(WriteWithdrawal(accountTbl,
freeMoneyTbl), &quot;WriteWithdrawal err&quot;)</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">	return
true</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">end</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">function
Main()</font>

  <font face="华文楷体, serif">--[[</font>

  <font face="华文楷体, serif">local
i = 1</font>

  <font face="华文楷体, serif">for
i = 1,#contract do</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">print(&quot;contract&quot;)</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">print(&quot;  &quot;,i,(contract[i]))	</font>

  <font face="华文楷体, serif">end</font>

  <font face="华文楷体, serif">--]]</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">assert(#contract &gt;= 2,&quot;contract
length err.&quot;)</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">assert(contract[1] == 0xff,&quot;Contract
identification error.&quot;)</font>

  <font face="华文楷体, serif">if
contract[2] == TX_TYPE.TX_RECHARGE then</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">assert(#contract == 60,&quot;recharge
contract length err.&quot;)</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">Recharge()	</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">elseif contract[2] == 
TX_TYPE.TX_WITHDRAW then</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">assert(#contract == 11,&quot;withdraw
contract length err.&quot;)</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">Withdraw(contract[3])</font>

  <font face="华文楷体, serif">else</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">error(&quot;RUN_SCRIPT_DATA_ERR&quot;)</font>

  <font face="华文楷体, serif">end</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">end</font>

<font face="华文楷体, serif">Main()</font>

<font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">以上面的示例代码为例，将其代码保存为</font></span></font><font face="华文楷体, serif">test.lua</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">，文件格式保存为</font></span></font><font face="华文楷体, serif">utf-8</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">：</font></span></font>

## <a name="__RefHeading__5559_848809181"></a><a name="_Toc464039830"></a>
5.1 <font face="华文楷体"><span lang="zh-CN">启动</span></font>dacrs<font face="华文楷体"><span lang="zh-CN">程序</span></font>

<font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">最好在</font></span></font><font face="华文楷体, serif">linux</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">下测试，</font></span></font><font face="华文楷体, serif">windows</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">上编译，调试慢。调试时先在</font></span></font><font face="华文楷体, serif">regtest</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">下调试通过，然后才在</font></span></font><font face="华文楷体, serif">testnet</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">和</font></span></font><font face="华文楷体, serif">main</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">网络上注册。</font></span></font>

<font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">修改</font></span></font><font face="华文楷体, serif">Dacrs.conf</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">文件，添加</font></span></font><font face="华文楷体, serif">regtest=1</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">，打开</font></span></font><font face="华文楷体, serif">vm</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">调试开关，</font></span></font><font face="华文楷体, serif">debug=vm</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">，注释掉</font></span></font><font face="华文楷体, serif">gen=1</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">，</font></span></font><font face="华文楷体, serif">genproclimit=1000000</font><font face="宋体"><span lang="zh-CN"><font face="华文楷体">，采用手动挖矿。</font></span></font>
